);

-- Order & sales KPIs
--- Total Orders
select count(Order_id) as "Total orders"
from `Tablename`;

---- total Revenue
select concat("$ ",sum(unit_Price * Quantity)) as "total Revenue"
from `tablename`;

--- Average order value
select concat("$ ",sum(unit_price * Quantity)/count(order_id) )as AOV
from `tablename`;

--- order by region
select Region,count(order_id) as total_orders
from `tablename`
group by Region
order by total_orders desc;

-- Inventory & stock KPIs
--- Stock on hand
select sum(stock_on_hand) 
from `tablename`;

--- Reorder_status_percentage
select (cast(sum(case WHEN Stock_On_Hand < Reorder_level Then 1 else 0 
end )AS decimal(10,2))  /count(*)) * 100 as Reorder_status_percentage
from `tablename`;

---- Average Lead time
select round( avg(lead_time_Days) ,2)as Avg_lead_time
from `tablename`;

-----  inventory turnover ratio
select round(sum((procurement_cost + transportation_cost) * Quantity )/ sum(stock_on_hand) , 2)as inventary_turnover_ratio
from `tablename`;

-- procurement & cost KPIs
--- Procurementcost
select sum(procurement_cost) as procurement_cost
from `tablename`;

---- transportation cost
select sum(transportation_cost) as transportation_cost
from `tablename`;

--- total supply chain cost
select sum((procurement_cost) * quantity) as Total_supplychain_cost
from `tablename`;

--- cost per unit
select concat("$ ",round(sum((procurement_cost) * quantity) / sum(quantity),2)) as cost_per_unit
from `tablename`;

-- logistics & delivary KPIs
---- Average Delay Days
select avg(Delay_Days) as Avg_delay_days
from `tablename`;

---- order by shipmode
select ship_mode,count(order_id) as total_orders
from `tablename`
group by Ship_Mode
order by total_orders desc;

---- transport mode utilization
select Transport_Mode,count(order_id) as total_orders
from `tablename`
group by Transport_Mode
order by total_orders desc;

-- On time delivery%
SELECT 
    (CAST(SUM(CASE WHEN Delivery_Status = 'On-Time' THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS FLOAT) 
     / COUNT(*)) * 100 AS On_Time_Delivery_Percentage
FROM 
    `tablename`;

-- Demand & fulfillment KPIs
-- forcast Accuracy
SELECT 
    AVG(1 - (ABS(- Forecast_Demand - Actual_Demand) / Forecast_Demand)) AS Forecast_Accuracy
FROM
    `tablename`;
    
-- Fill Rate
SELECT 
    AVG(Fill_Rate) AS fill_rate
FROM
    `tablename`;
    
-- Backorder date
SELECT 
    SUM(CASE
        WHEN Delivery_Status = 'Backordered' THEN 1
        ELSE 0
    END) / COUNT(*) AS Backorder_Rate_Percentage
FROM
    `tablename`;
    
    -- Demand vs Actual sales trend
SELECT 
    MONTHNAME(order_date),
    SUM(forecast_demand) AS Forecastdemand,
    SUM(Actual_demand) AS ActualDemand
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY MONTHNAME(order_date)
ORDER BY MONTHNAME(order_date);
SELECT 
    YEAR(order_date),
    SUM(forecast_demand) AS Forecastdemand,
    SUM(Actual_demand) AS ActualDemand
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY YEAR(order_date)
ORDER BY YEAR(order_date);
SELECT 
    *
FROM
    `tablename`;
 
 -- Delivary Status by region
SELECT 
    Delivery_Status, Region, COUNT(order_id) AS total_orders
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY region , Delivery_status
ORDER BY total_orders;
 
 -- Top suppliers by Procurement cost 
SELECT 
    supplier_id, procurement_cost
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY supplier_id , Procurement_Cost
ORDER BY Procurement_Cost DESC
LIMIT 10;
 
 -- transportation cost by transport mode
SELECT 
    transport_mode, transportation_cost
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY Transportation_Cost , Transport_Mode
ORDER BY Transportation_Cost DESC;
 
-- transportation cost trend over time
SELECT 
    DATE_FORMAT(order_date, '%y/%m') AS month,
    ROUND(SUM(transportation_cost), 2) AS transportation_cost
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY month
ORDER BY DATE_FORMAT(order_date, '%y/%m');

-- delay_days by ship mode
SELECT 
    Ship_Mode,
    AVG(delay_days) AS Delay_days,
    YEAR(order_date) AS order_date
FROM
    `tablename`
GROUP BY Ship_Mode , Order_Date
ORDER BY YEAR(order_date) DESC;
 
 -- Average Fill RAte
 select 
 round(avg(Fill_Rate),2) as Avg_fill_rate
 From tablename;
 
 -- Forecast error
 select
 sum(Actual_Demand)-sum(Forecast_Demand) as forecast_Error
 from
 `tablename`;
 
 -- forecast accuracy by region
 select Region,round(1 - (ABS(sum( Forecast_Demand )-sum( Actual_Demand) / nullif(sum(Forecast_Demand),2)))) AS Forecast_Accuracy
 from
 `tablename`
 group by Region;
 
 -- Transport_mode share by total shipments

 SELECT
    Transport_Mode,
    COUNT(*) AS Total_Shipments
FROM `tablename`
GROUP BY Transport_Mode;

-- Transportation Cost Trend over time
select round(sum( Transportation_Cost),2) as Transportation_cost, year(Order_Date) as order_date
from`tablename`
group by year(Order_Date)
order by year(Order_Date) desc;

-- - Transportation Cost by Transport_Mode
select Transport_Mode,round(sum(Transportation_Cost),2) as Transportation_cost
from `tablename`
group by Transport_Mode;

-- Procurement Cost by Lead Time 
select year(Order_Date) as order_date,round(sum(Procurement_Cost),2) as procurement_cost
from `tablename`
group by year(Order_Date)
order by year(Order_Date) desc;

-- Top Suppliers by Procurement Cost
select Supplier_Name,round(sum(Procurement_Cost),2) as procurement_cost
from `tablename`
group by Supplier_Name
order by procurement_cost desc;

-- Delay_Days by Ship_Mode
SELECT Ship_Mode,AVG(Delay_Days) AS DELAY_DAYS
FROM `tablename`
group by Ship_Mode;

--- COUNTRY WISE TOTAL SALES 
SELECT Country, concat("$ ",round(sum(unit_Price * Quantity),2)) as "total Revenue"
FROM `tablename`
group by Country
order by "TOTAL REVENUE";

-- top 10 products by sales
select `Product Name`,concat("$ ",sum(unit_Price * Quantity)) as "total sales"
from `tablename`
group by  `Product Name`
order by  concat("$ ",sum(unit_Price * Quantity)) desc
limit 10;
